local function CRQDKY_fake_script() 
	local script = Instance.new('Script', Credits)

	local credits = script.Parent
	local text
	
	function SoundEffect ()
		local Sound = Instance.new("Sound",Workspace)
		Sound.Name = "TextSound"
		Sound.SoundId = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=8042877195"
		Sound.PlaybackSpeed = 1
		Sound.Volume = 0.2
		Sound:Play()
		coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
			wait(1)
			Sound:Destroy()
		end))
	end
	
	function setText(word)
		text = word
		for i = 1, #text do
			credits.Text = string.sub(text, 1, i)
			SoundEffect()
			wait(0.04)
		end
	end
	
	
	setText("loading its pretty fast doe")
end
coroutine.wrap(CRQDKY_fake_script)()
wait(3)
MainFrame:Destroy()
Credits:Destroy()

local function CRQDKY_fake_script() 
	local script = Instance.new('Script', Credits)

	local credits = script.Parent
	local text
	
	function SoundEffect ()
		local Sound = Instance.new("Sound",Workspace)
		Sound.Name = "TextSound"
		Sound.SoundId = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=8042877195"
		Sound.PlaybackSpeed = 20
		Sound.Volume = 0.6
		Sound:Play()
		coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
			wait(1)
			Sound:Destroy()
		end))
	end
	
	function setText(word)
		text = word
		for i = 1, #text do
			credits.Text = string.sub(text, 1, i)
			SoundEffect()
			wait(0.003)
		end
	end
	
	
	setText("*Now Playing an ordinary megalovania")
end

char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
function effect(name,offset,color,s,rotation) -- name is the name of the effect in replicatedstorage.Effects, offset is a cframe value offset from where you are, S is a size increase, rotation rotates the effect by another cframe
    local effect = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Effects[name]:Clone()
    effect.Parent = char
    --effect.CFrame = char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame*CFrame.new(0,15,0)
    for _,v in pairs(effect:GetDescendants()) do
        spawn(function()
            Angle = rotation
            v.CFrame = char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame*offset*Angle
        end)
        spawn(function()
            v.Color = color
        end)
        spawn(function()
            v.Size = v.Size*s
        end)
    end
end



    effect("SpeedLines", CFrame.new(Vector3.new(0,0,0)), ColorSequence.new(Color3.new(0, 0, 0),Color3.new(0, 0, 0)) , 0, CFrame.Angles(math.rad(1000),0,0))

local radius = 7 --how far away do you want the parts to be from you
local circle = math.pi * 15-- Gets a full circle
local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
local tab = {}--Creates a table so you can insert values inside
local amm = 6 ---amount of projectiles
pass = getrenv()._G.Pass
for i = 1,amm,1 do
spawn(function()
local A_1 =  {
     [1] = pass, 
     [2] = "KnifeProjectileYellow", 
     [3] = "Spawn", 
     [4] = (char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame*CFrame.new(1,100,-10)).p
}
local Event = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.CharaMoves
Event:InvokeServer(A_1)
end)
end
am = 0
local detect
local detect2
val = Instance.new('NumberValue',player)-- creates a value instance so you can use it in a connect function
val.Name = 'YellowOrb Count'
detect = char.Attacks.ChildAdded:Connect(function(pp)-- this will detect if a child is added to the character
if pp.Name == 'YellowBlast' then
    table.insert(tab,pp)--it will insert the blasts to the table
am = am + 1--adds the numbers
val.Value = am--set the Number value to that number
pp:WaitForChild('BodyVelocity'):Destroy()
pp:WaitForChild('Hitted'):Destroy()
pp:WaitForChild('Particle'):WaitForChild('ParticleEmitter'):Destroy()
pp:WaitForChild('Trial'):Destroy()
pp:WaitForChild('Particlex'):Destroy()
end
end)

detect2 = val:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Value"):Connect(function()-- detects if the value is equal to the amount of time the remote is fired
if val.Value == amm then
tab2 = {}
for _,v in pairs(tab) do---will look through the tables
v.CFrame = char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame*CFrame.new(math.random(-20,20),1000,math.random(-20,20))
v1 = Instance.new('BodyPosition',v)
fol = Instance.new('Folder',v1)
v1.Name = 'Client'
v1.MaxForce = Vector3.new(1,1,1)*100000
v1.D = 500
v1.P = 30000
v1.Position = (char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame).p + Vector3.new(0,0,0)
        table.insert(tab2,v1)
end



for i = 1,#tab2 do
spawn(function()
local angle = circle / #tab2 * i---this will get the amount of parts you have and multiply with the current i to get the proper postion to make a circle
    local part = tab2[i]
local  mspeed = 0
while true do
    wait()
    mspeed = mspeed + 1500-- change it to a higher number if u want it faster
    local x_pos = math.cos(angle) * radius
    local y_pos = math.sin(angle) * radius
    local cf = char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(100), math.rad(mspeed),math.rad(0)) *CFrame.new(x_pos, 0, y_pos)
part.Position = cf.p
end
end)
end
val:Destroy()
detect:Disconnect()
detect2:Disconnect()
end
end)

local speeds = {999,999}--put as many speeds as how much projectile you have (in order)
for i = 1,#tab2 do
spawn(function()
local angle = circle / #tab2 * i---this will get the amount of parts you have and multiply with the current i to get the proper postion to make a circle
local add = speeds[i]
    local part = tab2[i]
local  mspeed = 0
while true do
    wait()
    mspeed = mspeed + 2000 -- change it to a higher number if u want it faster
    local x_pos = math.cos(angle) * radius
    local y_pos = math.sin(angle) * radius
    local cf = char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(100), math.rad(mspeed),math.rad(20)) *CFrame.new(x_pos, 0, y_pos)
part.Position = cf.p
end
end)
end
val:Destroy()
detect:Disconnect()
detect2:Disconnect()
end
end)
char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
function effect(name,offset,color,s,rotation) -- name is the name of the effect in replicatedstorage.Effects, offset is a cframe value offset from where you are, S is a size increase, rotation rotates the effect by another cframe
    local effect = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Effects[name]:Clone()
    effect.Parent = char
    --effect.CFrame = char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame*CFrame.new(0,15,0)
    for _,v in pairs(effect:GetDescendants()) do
        spawn(function()
            Angle = rotation
            v.CFrame = char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame*offset*Angle
        end)
        spawn(function()
            v.Color = color
        end)
        spawn(function()
            v.Size = v.Size*s
        end)
    end
end



    effect("SpeedLines", CFrame.new(Vector3.new(0,0,0)), ColorSequence.new(Color3.new(0, 0, 0),Color3.new(0, 0, 0)) , 0, CFrame.Angles(math.rad(1000),0,0))

local detect
local detect2
val = Instance.new('NumberValue',player)-- creates a value instance so you can use it in a connect function
val.Name = 'YellowOrb Count'
detect = char.Attacks.ChildAdded:Connect(function(pp)-- this will detect if a child is added to the character
if pp.Name == 'YellowBlast' then
    table.insert(tab,pp)--it will insert the blasts to the table
am = am + 1--adds the numbers
val.Value = am--set the Number value to that number
pp:WaitForChild('BodyVelocity'):Destroy()
pp:WaitForChild('Hitted'):Destroy()
end
end)

detect2 = val:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Value"):Connect(function()-- detects if the value is equal to the amount of time the remote is fired
if val.Value == amm then
tab2 = {}
for _,v in pairs(tab) do---will look through the tables
v.CFrame = char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame*CFrame.new(math.random(-20,20),1000,math.random(-20,20))
v1 = Instance.new('BodyPosition',v)
fol = Instance.new('Folder',v1)
v1.Name = 'Client'
v1.MaxForce = Vector3.new(1,1,1)*100000
v1.D = 500
v1.P = 30000
v1.Position = (char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame).p + Vector3.new(0,0,0)
        table.insert(tab2,v1)
end



for i = 1,#tab2 do
spawn(function()
local angle = circle / #tab2 * i---this will get the amount of parts you have and multiply with the current i to get the proper postion to make a circle
    local part = tab2[i]
local  mspeed = 0
while true do
    wait()
    mspeed = mspeed + 14-- change it to a higher number if u want it faster
    local x_pos = math.cos(angle) * radius
    local y_pos = math.sin(angle) * radius
    local cf = char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(100), math.rad(mspeed),math.rad(0)) *CFrame.new(x_pos, 2, y_pos)
part.Position = cf.p
end
end)
end
val:Destroy()
detect:Disconnect()
detect2:Disconnect()
end
end)

local plr = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer
local c = plr.Character
function tp() --makes the tp function
local LockOn = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack.Main.LockOnScript.LockOn.Value
if not LockOn then 
             root = c.HumanoidRootPart
             rcf = root.CFrame - root.Position
             mo = plr:GetMouse()
             pos = CFrame.new(mo.Hit.p)*rcf
    tar = pos
    c.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = tar
elseif LockOn then
    target = LockOn
    tar = target.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0,0,-4)
    c.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = tar
end
end
local mouse = game.Players.LocalPlayer:GetMouse()
mouse.KeyDown:Connect(function(k)
    if k == "b" then 
tp()
wait(0.2)
game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack.Main.LockOnScript.LockOn.Value
game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraType = "Orbital"
                   local A_1 = getrenv()._G.Pass
                    local A_2 = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack.Main.LockOnScript.LockOn.Value
                    local A_3 = {
                        ["HitTime"] = 1.7, --the amount of time the remote is hitting the enemy for (it cant be over one or 0)
                        ["Type"] = "Knockback", --the type of thing it is like knockback and normal (Knockback and Normal are the only usable types)
                        ["HitEffect"] = "HeavyHitEffect", --This is the effect of ur hit I'll explain more about this later
                        ["HurtAnimation"] = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Animations.HurtAnimations.Knockback1, --this is the animation of ur enemy when hurt
                        ["Sound"] = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Sounds.Kick,
                        ["CameraShake"] = "BigExplosion", --how much ur screen shakes! you can pick from (Bump and BigExplosion I forgot the others)
                        ["Velocity"] = Vector3.new(0,35,0) + game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.lookVector * 50,
                        ["BlockAble"] = false,
                        ["CombatInv"] = true, --always keep this on so u can do stuff
                        ["Damage"] = 4 --amount of dmg ur attack does Knockback remotes can do 0-40 dmg while Normal does 0-20

                    }
                local Event = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.Damage
				Event:InvokeServer(A_1, A_2, A_3)
wait(1)
		        char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character -- self explanatory
char.Humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Flying) -- sets yourself into a flying state
tar = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Backpack.Main.LockOnScript.LockOn.Value.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame*CFrame.new(0,1,50)
char.Humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Flying)
v2 = Instance.new('BodyPosition',char.HumanoidRootPart) -- creates the bodypos
fol = Instance.new('Folder',v2)---adding folder instance so it can be 'Whitelisted'
v2.Name = 'Client' -- names the bodypos so it doesnt crash you
v2.MaxForce = Vector3.new(1,1,1)*100000 -- the max force, dont touch
v2.D = 1000 -- the dampening, so basically how much it slows down before you get to your destination
v2.P = 50000 -- the power, or how fast you go
v2.Position = (tar).p -- sets the bodypos destination
char.Humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Jumping)
wait(0.4)
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Anchored = true
wait(0.2)

                   local A_1 = getrenv()._G.Pass
                    local A_2 = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack.Main.LockOnScript.LockOn.Value
                    local A_3 = {
                        ["HitTime"] = 1.7, --the amount of time the remote is hitting the enemy for (it cant be over one or 0)
                        ["Type"] = "Knockback", --the type of thing it is like knockback and normal (Knockback and Normal are the only usable types)
                        ["HitEffect"] = "HeavyHitEffect", --This is the effect of ur hit I'll explain more about this later

spawn(function()
	local lol = Instance.new('Color3Value')
	lol.Parent = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Character.Bracelets
	lol.Name = 'yee'
	lol.Value = Color3.fromHSV(0.725,1,1) -- tween to 0.8
	spawn(function()
		local ti = TweenInfo.new(
			2.5, -- Time
			Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, -- EasingStyle
			Enum.EasingDirection.InOut, -- EasingDirection
			-1, -- RepeatCount (when less than zero the tween will loop indefinitely)
			true, -- Reverses (tween will reverse once reaching it's goal)
			0.5 -- DelayTime
		)

		local tween1 = game:GetService('TweenService'):Create(lol, ti, {Value = Color3.fromHSV(0.8,1,1)})
		tween1:Play()
	end)

if not (getgc and getconstants and setconstant) then
    
    warn("NOT SUPPORTED EXPLOIT")
    game.StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
    	Title = "WARNING";
    	Text = "NOT SUPPORTED EXPLOIT";
    	Duration = 5;
    })
    return
    
end

pcall(function()
    
    local funcs = {}
    
    for i, v in next, getgc() do
        
        if type(v) == "function" then
            
            if getfenv(v).script and getfenv(v).script.Name and getfenv(v).script.Name == "LockOnScript" then
                
                table.insert(funcs, v)
                
            end
            
        end
        
    end
    
    repeat wait() until #funcs ~= 0
    
    local target = funcs[#funcs]
    
    for i2, v2 in next, getconstants(target) do
        
        if i2 == 44 and tostring(v2) == "0" then
            
            setconstant(target, i2, -999999)
            print("hooked")
            
        end
        
    end
    
end)
end
end)

local slashes = {}
game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Character:WaitForChild("Attacks").ChildAdded:Connect(function(child) 
    if child.Name == "YellowBlast" then 
        child:WaitForChild("Hitted"):Destroy()
        child:WaitForChild("Particle"):Destroy()
        table.insert(slashes,child) 
        print(child.Name)
    end
end)
wait(1)
local rs = game:GetService("RunService")
i = 1
local target1 = slashes[1]
local Parts = {Part1, Part2, Part3, Part4, Part5, Part6, Part7}
rs.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
	target1.CFrame = Parts[i].CFrame
	i = i + 1
	if i == 8 then i = 1 end
end)
i2 = 1
local target2 = slashes[2]
local Parts2 = {Partt1, Partt2, Partt3, Partt4, Partt5, Partt6, Partt7}
rs.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
	target2.CFrame = Parts2[i2].CFrame
	i2 = i2 + 1
	if i2 == 8 then i2 = 1 end
end)
i3 = 1
local target3 = slashes[3]
local Parts3 = {lolz1, lolz2, lolz3, lolz4, lolz5, lolz6, lolz7}
rs.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
	target3.CFrame = Parts3[i2].CFrame
	i3 = i3 + 1
	if i3 == 8 then i3 = 1 end
end)
end
end)
local mouse = game.Players.LocalPlayer:GetMouse()
mouse.KeyDown:Connect(function(k)
    if k == "e" then 
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Attacks:ClearAllChildren()
_G.cdr = false
if _G.cdr then return end
_G.cdr = true
pass = getrenv()._G.Pass
player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
m = player:GetMouse()
local LockOn = player.Backpack.Main.LockOnScript.LockOn.Value
if LockOn then 
target = LockOn
r2 = target.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
elseif not LockOn then
r2 = m.Hit*CFrame.new(0,5,0)
end
char = player.Character
h = char.Humanoid
a = Instance.new('Animation')
a.AnimationId = 'rbxassetid://4905914802'

k:Play()

      [4] = r2.p

end)
end
am = 0
val = Instance.new('NumberValue',player)
val.Name = 'KnifeSlashes Amount'
local tabeeas = {}
detect = char.Attacks.ChildAdded:Connect(function(pp)
if pp.Name == 'KnifeSlashProjectileDark' then
    table.insert(tabeeas,pp)
    spawn(function()
   local rp
   local yeaeoase = pp
rp = yeaeoase.Changed:Connect(function(pr)
    if pr == "Anchored" then
if not pr.Anchored then
am = am + 1
val.Value = am
rp:Disconnect()
end
    end
end)
end)
end
end)
detect2 = val:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Value"):Connect(function()
if val.Value == amm*3 then
tab = {}
tab2 = {}
for _,v in pairs(char.Attacks:GetChildren()) do
if v.Name == 'KnifeSlashProjectileDark' then
    v:WaitForChild('BodyVelocity'):Destroy()
    v:WaitForChild('ParticleEmitter'):Destroy()
    v:WaitForChild('Burst'):Destroy()
v.CFrame = char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame*CFrame.new(0,10,-2)
v1 = Instance.new('BodyPosition',v)
fol = Instance.new('Folder',v1)
v1.Name = 'Client'
v1.MaxForce = Vector3.new(1,1,1)*100000
v1.D = 100
v1.P = 300000
v2 = Instance.new('BodyGyro',v)
fol = Instance.new('Folder',v2)
v2.Name = 'Client'
v2.MaxTorque = Vector3.new(1,1,1)*10000
v2.D = 1000
v2.P = 5000
v2.CFrame = char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0),0,0)
x = math.random(0,0)*2
z = math.random(0,0)*2
v1.Position = (char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame).p + Vector3.new(0,10,15)
table.insert(tab,v1)
table.insert(tab2,v)
v1.Position = (char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame).p + Vector3.new(x,500,z)
end
end
wait(.5)
for i = 1,#tab do
    m.TargetFilter = game.workspace.Terrain
local LockOn = player.Backpack.Main.LockOnScript.LockOn.Value
if LockOn then 
target = LockOn
r2 = target.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
r1 = target.HumanoidRootPart
elseif not LockOn then
r2 = m.Hit
r1 = m.Target
end
x = math.random(-669,669)
z = math.random(50,50)
tab[i].D = 150
tab[i].Position = r2.p + Vector3.new(0,0,0)
tab2[i].CFrame = r2*CFrame.new(x,100,z)
spawn(function()
local A_1 =  {
      [1] = pass, 
      [2] = "KnifeProjectileDarkRed", 
      [3] = "Hit", 
      [4] = tab2[i], 
      [5] = r2, 
      [6] = r1
}
local Event = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.CharaMoves
Event:InvokeServer(A_1)
end)
wait()
end
end
end)
wait(15)
for _,v in pairs(tabeeas) do
    v:Destroy()
    end
detect:Disconnect()
detect2:Disconnect()
val:Destroy()
_G.cdr = false
end
end)
local plr = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer--hey! look down and look at the instructions
local c = plr.Character --to make it function! (continuation of the top)
function tp() --makes the tp function
local LockOn = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack.Main.LockOnScript.LockOn.Value
if not LockOn then 
             root = c.HumanoidRootPart
             rcf = root.CFrame - root.Position
             mo = plr:GetMouse()
             pos = CFrame.new(mo.Hit.p)*rcf
    tar = pos
    c.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = tar
elseif LockOn then
    target = LockOn
    tar = target.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0,0,-4)
    c.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = tar
end
end
local plr = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer
local c = plr.Character
function top() --makes the tp function
local LockOn = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack.Main.LockOnScript.LockOn.Value
if not LockOn then 
             root = c.HumanoidRootPart
             rcf = root.CFrame - root.Position
             mo = plr:GetMouse()
             pos = CFrame.new(mo.Hit.p)*rcf
    tar = pos
    c.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = tar
elseif LockOn then
    target = LockOn
    tar = target.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0,0,4)
    c.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = tar
end
end

    c.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = tar
end
